Request Description
StartFragment This POST request handles user authentication by validating credentials against the `DummyJSON` server. It is the most critical part of the sauce demo workflow because it generates the `accessToken` required for all subsequent "Authorized" API calls (like Cart and Checkout). ## Technical Details - **Method:** `POST` - **Endpoint:** `https://dummyjson.com/auth/login` - **Body:** JSON (Username/Password) ## QA Testing Logic (Automated Scripts) I have implemented a suite of **Postman Tests** to verify the response quality. You can see the results in the **Test Results (5/5)** tab. The logic covers: - **Basic Connectivity:** Checks if the status is exactly `200 OK`. - **Performance Benchmark:** Verifies the response time is under `1000ms` to ensure a smooth user experience. - **Identity Verification:** Specifically checks if the `username` returned is `emilys` and the email contains the correct domain. - **Auth Security:** Confirms that the `accessToken` is a valid string and not empty before saving it to the environment. - **Data Structure (Schema):** A strict check on the JSON keys (id, email, gender, etc.) to catch any breaking changes in the backend response. ## Compliance & Rules EndFragment

Request Description
# Filter Users by Attribute This endpoint allows you to filter users based on specific attributes and their corresponding values. In this example, the endpoint filters users by gender to retrieve only female users. ## Query Parameters | Parameter | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `key` | string | Yes | The attribute name to filter by (e.g., `gender`, `age`, `bloodGroup`, etc.) | | `value` | string | Yes | The value to match for the specified key (e.g., `female`, `male`, etc.) | ## How It Works The filtering mechanism uses a key-value pair approach: - **key**: Specifies which user attribute to filter on - **value**: Specifies what value that attribute should match For example: - `key=gender&value=female` returns all female users - `key=gender&value=male` would return all male users - Other filterable attributes may include age, bloodGroup, eyeColor, etc. ## Response Structure The endpoint returns a JSON object containing: ``` json { "users": [ { "id": 1, "firstName": "string", "lastName": "string", "maidenName": "string", "age": number, "gender": "string", "email": "string", "phone": "string", "username": "string", "birthDate": "string", "image": "string", "bloodGroup": "string", "height": number, "weight": number, "eyeColor": "string", "hair": { "color": "string", "type": "string" }, "ip": "string", "address": { "address": "string", "city": "string", "state": "string", "stateCode": "string", "postalCode": "string", "coordinates": { "lat": number, "lng": number }, "country": "string" }, "macAddress": "string", "university": "string", "bank": { "cardExpire": "string", "cardNumber": "string", "cardType": "string", "currency": "string", "iban": "string" }, "company": { "department": "string", "name": "string", "title": "string", "address": { ... } }, "ein": "string", "ssn": "string", "userAgent": "string", "crypto": { "coin": "string", "wallet": "string", "network": "string" }, "role": "string" } ] } ``` ## Response Fields Each user object includes comprehensive information: - **Personal Information**: firstName, lastName, age, gender, birthDate, email, phone - **Physical Attributes**: height, weight, eyeColor, bloodGroup, hair details - **Contact Details**: address with coordinates, phone, email - **Financial Information**: bank card details, currency, IBAN - **Professional Details**: company information, department, job title - **Security**: username, SSN, EIN - **Additional**: university, IP address, MAC address, crypto wallet, user role ## Expected Response - **Status Code**: `200 OK` - **Content-Type**: `application/json` ## Notes - The filter returns all users that match the specified criteria - The response includes complete user profiles with all available attributes - The `bank.currency` field is guaranteed to exist in the response (validated by tests) - All returned users will have the `gender` field matching the filter value (validated by tests) - This endpoint is useful for segmenting users by demographic or other attributes for analysis or targeted operations

It accepts user details in the request body and returns the complete user object with a generated ID upon successful creation. ## Request Details **Endpoint:** `POST https://dummyjson.com/users/add` **Method:** `POST` **Content-Type:** `application/json` ## Request Body Parameters The request body should contain the following fields: | Parameter | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `firstName` | string | Yes | The user's first name | | `lastName` | string | Yes | The user's last name | | `age` | integer | Yes | The user's age | | `email` | string | Yes | The user's email address | | `gender` | string | Yes | The user's gender (e.g., "male", "female") | ### Example Request Body ``` json { "firstName": "Noor", "lastName": "janajreh", "age": 22, "email": "noor.janajreh@htu.edu.jo", "gender": "female" } ``` ## Response ### Success Response **Status Code:** `201 Created` The response includes the newly created user object with all fields populated, including: - `id`: Auto-generated unique identifier for the user - All submitted fields (`firstName`, `lastName`, `age`, `email`, `gender`) - Additional user properties with default/empty values (e.g., `phone`, `address`, `company`, `bank`, etc.) ### Example Response ``` json { "id": 209, "firstName": "Noor", "lastName": "janajreh", "age": 22, "gender": "female", "email": "noor.janajreh@htu.edu.jo", "role": "user", ... } ``` ## Notes - The API automatically generates a unique `id` for each new user - Additional user properties (address, company, bank details, etc.) are initialized with empty or null values - The default role assigned to new users is "user" - Ensure all required fields are provided to avoid validation errors

Request Description
# Update User Profile ## Overview This endpoint updates a specific user's profile information by their unique user ID. It allows partial updates to user data while returning the complete user profile with all personal, professional, and financial information. ## Request Details **Method:** `PUT` **URL:** `https://dummyjson.com/users/{id}` **Path Parameters:** - `id` (integer, required) - The unique identifier of the user to update (e.g., `1`) ## Request Body The request accepts a JSON object with the fields you want to update. You can send partial updates - only the fields you include will be modified. **Format:** `application/json` **Example Request Body:** ``` json { "lastName": "janajreh" } ``` **Available Fields for Update:** - `firstName` (string) - User's first name - `lastName` (string) - User's last name - `age` (integer) - User's age - `email` (string) - User's email address - `phone` (string) - User's phone number - `role` (string) - User's role (e.g., "admin", "user") - Additional fields as supported by the API ## Response **Success Status Code:** `200 OK` The response returns the complete user profile with all fields, including those that were not updated. **Response Body Structure:** ``` json { "id": 1, "firstName": "Emily", "lastName": "janajreh", "maidenName": "Smith", "age": 29, "gender": "female", "email": "emily.johnson@x.dummyjson.com", "phone": "+81 965-431-3024", "username": "emilys", "password": "emilyspass", "birthDate": "1996-5-30", "image": "https://dummyjson.com/icon/emilys/128", "bloodGroup": "O-", "height": 193.24, "weight": 63.16, "eyeColor": "Green", "hair": { "color": "Brown", "type": "Curly" }, "address": { "address": "626 Main Street", "city": "Phoenix", "state": "Mississippi", "stateCode": "MS", "postalCode": "29112", "coordinates": { "lat": -77.16213, "lng": -92.084824 }, "country": "United States" }, "company": { "department": "Engineering", "name": "Dooley, Kozey and Cronin", "title": "Sales Manager", "address": { ... } }, "bank": { "cardExpire": "05/28", "cardNumber": "3693233511855044", "cardType": "Diners Club International", "currency": "GBP", "iban": "GB74MH2UZLR9TRPHYNU8F8" }, "role": "admin" } ``` ## Response Data Categories The complete response includes: ### Personal Information - Basic identity: `firstName`, `lastName`, `maidenName`, `username` - Demographics: `age`, `gender`, `birthDate` - Contact: `email`, `phone` - Profile: `image`, `password` ### Physical Attributes - `height` (number) - Height in cm - `weight` (number) - Weight in kg - `eyeColor` (string) - Eye color - `bloodGroup` (string) - Blood type - `hair` (object) - Hair color and type ### Address Information - Complete address with street, city, state, postal code - Geographic coordinates (latitude/longitude) - Country information ### Employment Details - `company.department` - Department name - `company.name` - Company name - `company.title` - Job title - `company.address` - Company address ### Financial Information - `bank.cardType` - Credit card type - `bank.cardNumber` - Card number - `bank.cardExpire` - Expiration date - `bank.currency` - Currency code - `bank.iban` - International bank account number ### System Information - `role` - User role/permissions level - `id` - Unique user identifier - Additional metadata: `ip`, `macAddress`, `userAgent`, `ein`, `ssn`, `crypto` ## Status Codes - **200 OK** - User successfully updated, returns complete user profile - **400 Bad Request** - Invalid request body or parameters - **401 Unauthorized** - Authentication required or failed - **404 Not Found** - User with specified ID does not exist - **500 Internal Server Error** - Server error occurred ## Authentication Authentication requirements depend on your API configuration. Ensure proper authentication headers are included if required. ## Important Notes - This endpoint performs a **partial update** - only fields included in the request body are modified - The response always returns the **complete user profile** regardless of which fields were updated - The `id` in the URL path must match an existing user - All data types must be valid (e.g., numbers for height/weight, valid email format) - The endpoint is used for testing that user data integrity is maintained across updates - Sensitive information like passwords and financial data are included in the response ## Automated Tests This request includes automated tests that verify: Response status is 200 User identity fields are correct (firstName, lastName, role) Physical attributes match expected values Data types are valid (height/weight are numbers, email format) Employment information is accurate Bank currency and card information is present

Request Description
# Delete User by ID ## Overview This endpoint performs a **soft delete** operation on a user account. Instead of permanently removing the user record from the database, it marks the user as deleted by setting the `isDeleted` flag to `true` and recording the deletion timestamp in `deletedOn`. ## Endpoint Details **Method:** `DELETE` **URL:** `https://dummyjson.com/users/{id}` ## Path Parameters | Parameter | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `id` | integer | Yes | The unique identifier of the user to delete. Example: `1` | ## Request Example ``` http DELETE https://dummyjson.com/users/1 ``` ## Response ### Success Response **Status Code:** `200 OK` The endpoint returns the complete user object with deletion metadata appended. **Response Body Structure:** ``` json { "id": 1, "firstName": "Emily", "lastName": "Johnson", "maidenName": "Smith", "age": 29, "gender": "female", "email": "emily.johnson@x.dummyjson.com", "phone": "+81 965-431-3024", "username": "emilys", "password": "emilyspass", "birthDate": "1996-5-30", "image": "https://dummyjson.com/icon/emilys/128", "bloodGroup": "O-", "height": 193.24, "weight": 63.16, "eyeColor": "Green", "hair": { "color": "Brown", "type": "Curly" }, "address": { "address": "626 Main Street", "city": "Phoenix", "state": "Mississippi", "stateCode": "MS", "postalCode": "29112", "coordinates": { "lat": -77.16213, "lng": -92.084824 }, "country": "United States" }, "university": "University of Wisconsin--Madison", "bank": { "cardExpire": "05/28", "cardNumber": "3693233511855044", "cardType": "Diners Club International", "currency": "GBP", "iban": "GB74MH2UZLR9TRPHYNU8F8" }, "company": { "department": "Engineering", "name": "Dooley, Kozey and Cronin", "title": "Sales Manager", "address": { "address": "263 Tenth Street", "city": "San Francisco", "state": "Wisconsin", "stateCode": "WI", "postalCode": "37657", "coordinates": { "lat": 71.814525, "lng": -161.150263 }, "country": "United States" } }, "ein": "977-175", "ssn": "900-590-289", "userAgent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Macintosh; Intel Mac OS X 10_15_7)...", "crypto": { "coin": "Bitcoin", "wallet": "0xb9fc2fe63b2a6c003f1c324c3bfa53259162181a", "network": "Ethereum (ERC20)" }, "role": "admin", "isDeleted": true, "deletedOn": "2026-01-28T23:25:05.460Z" } ``` ### Key Response Fields | Field | Type | Description | | --- | --- | --- | | `id` | integer | The unique identifier of the deleted user | | `isDeleted` | boolean | Deletion status flag. Will be `true` after successful deletion | | `deletedOn` | string (ISO 8601) | Timestamp indicating when the user was deleted | | _(all other fields)_ | various | Complete user profile data is retained in the response | ## Deletion Behavior ### Soft Delete This endpoint implements a **soft delete** strategy: - User record remains in the database - `isDeleted` flag is set to `true` - `deletedOn` timestamp is recorded - All user data is preserved - User can potentially be restored later - User record is NOT permanently removed ### Benefits of Soft Delete - **Data Recovery:** Deleted users can be restored if needed - **Audit Trail:** Maintains historical records for compliance - **Referential Integrity:** Preserves relationships with other entities - **Analytics:** Deleted user data remains available for reporting ## Status Codes | Status Code | Description | | --- | --- | | `200 OK` | User successfully marked as deleted | | `404 Not Found` | User with the specified ID does not exist | | `401 Unauthorized` | Authentication required or invalid credentials | | `403 Forbidden` | Insufficient permissions to delete users | ## Automated Tests This request includes automated tests that verify: 1. Response status code is `200` 2. Response time is less than 1000ms 3. User deletion is confirmed (`isDeleted` is `true`) ## Notes - The complete user object is returned in the response, allowing you to verify which user was deleted - The `deletedOn` field uses ISO 8601 format with timezone information - Consider implementing additional business logic to handle deleted users in your application (e.g., filtering them from user lists, preventing login, etc.) - If you need to permanently remove user data (hard delete), a different endpoint may be required

Request Description
## Overview This endpoint retrieves a paginated list of products from the catalog. It returns comprehensive product information including pricing, inventory, ratings, reviews, and media assets. ## Response Structure The response returns a JSON object containing an array of product objects with detailed information about each item. ### Response Fields | Field | Type | Description | | --- | --- | --- | | `products` | Array | Array of product objects | ### Product Object Fields #### Basic Information - **id** (number): Unique product identifier - **title** (string): Product name/title - **description** (string): Detailed product description - **category** (string): Product category (e.g., "beauty", "fragrances") - **brand** (string): Brand name - **sku** (string): Stock Keeping Unit identifier - **tags** (array): Array of product tags for categorization #### Pricing & Discounts - **price** (number): Current product price - **discountPercentage** (number): Percentage discount applied #### Inventory & Availability - **stock** (number): Available quantity in stock - **availabilityStatus** (string): Current availability status (e.g., "In Stock") - **minimumOrderQuantity** (number): Minimum quantity required for order #### Ratings & Reviews - **rating** (number): Average product rating - **reviews** (array): Array of review objects containing: - `rating` (number): Individual review rating - `comment` (string): Review text - `date` (string): Review date in ISO format - `reviewerName` (string): Name of reviewer - `reviewerEmail` (string): Email of reviewer #### Physical Attributes - **weight** (number): Product weight - **dimensions** (object): Product dimensions containing: - `width` (number) - `height` (number) - `depth` (number) #### Policies & Shipping - **warrantyInformation** (string): Warranty details - **shippingInformation** (string): Shipping timeframe and details - **returnPolicy** (string): Return policy information #### Media Assets - **images** (array): Array of product image URLs - **thumbnail** (string): Thumbnail image URL #### Metadata - **meta** (object): Additional metadata containing: - `createdAt` (string): Creation timestamp - `updatedAt` (string): Last update timestamp - `barcode` (string): Product barcode - `qrCode` (string): QR code URL ## Usage Notes - This endpoint returns multiple products in a single response - Products span multiple categories (beauty, fragrances, etc.) - Each product includes comprehensive review data with multiple customer reviews - All timestamps are in ISO 8601 format - Image URLs are provided as full CDN paths - The response includes both essential product data and extended metadata for comprehensive product management

Request Description
## Overview This endpoint allows you to search for products in the catalog using a search query. It returns a list of products that match the search term, including detailed information about each product. ## Endpoint ``` GET https://dummyjson.com/products/search ``` ## Query Parameters | Parameter | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `q` | string | Yes | The search term to find products. Searches across product titles, descriptions, categories, and other relevant fields. | ### Example Query Parameters - `q=phone` - Search for products related to "phone" - `q=laptop` - Search for laptop products - `q=apple` - Search for Apple brand products ## Response Format The endpoint returns a JSON object containing an array of matching products. ### Response Structure ``` json { "products": [ { "id": 101, "title": "Apple AirPods Max Silver", "description": "Product description text...", "category": "mobile-accessories", "price": 549.99, "discountPercentage": 13.67, "rating": 3.47, "stock": 59, "tags": ["electronics", "over-ear headphones"], "brand": "Apple", "sku": "MOB-APP-APP-101", "weight": 2, "dimensions": { "width": 24.88, "height": 14.9, "depth": 27.54 }, "warrantyInformation": "No warranty", "shippingInformation": "Ships in 2 weeks", "availabilityStatus": "In Stock", "reviews": [ { "rating": 5, "comment": "Excellent quality!", "date": "2025-04-30T09:41:02.053Z", "reviewerName": "Henry Adams", "reviewerEmail": "henry.adams@x.dummyjson.com" } ], "returnPolicy": "No return policy", "minimumOrderQuantity": 1, "meta": { "createdAt": "2025-04-30T09:41:02.053Z", "updatedAt": "2025-04-30T09:41:02.053Z", "barcode": "4062176053732", "qrCode": "https://cdn.dummyjson.com/public/qr-code..." }, "images": [ "https://cdn.dummyjson.com/product-images/..." ], "thumbnail": "https://cdn.dummyjson.com/product-images/..." } ], "total": 10, "skip": 0, "limit": 30 } ``` ### Response Fields | Field | Type | Description | | --- | --- | --- | | `products` | array | Array of product objects matching the search query | | `products[].id` | integer | Unique product identifier | | `products[].title` | string | Product name/title | | `products[].description` | string | Detailed product description | | `products[].category` | string | Product category | | `products[].price` | number | Product price in USD | | `products[].discountPercentage` | number | Current discount percentage | | `products[].rating` | number | Average customer rating (0-5) | | `products[].stock` | integer | Available stock quantity | | `products[].tags` | array | Product tags for categorization | | `products[].brand` | string | Product brand name | | `products[].sku` | string | Stock Keeping Unit identifier | | `products[].weight` | number | Product weight | | `products[].dimensions` | object | Product dimensions (width, height, depth) | | `products[].warrantyInformation` | string | Warranty details | | `products[].shippingInformation` | string | Shipping timeframe | | `products[].availabilityStatus` | string | Stock availability status | | `products[].reviews` | array | Customer reviews with ratings and comments | | `products[].returnPolicy` | string | Return policy information | | `products[].minimumOrderQuantity` | integer | Minimum quantity required for order | | `products[].meta` | object | Metadata including creation date, barcode, QR code | | `products[].images` | array | Array of product image URLs | | `products[].thumbnail` | string | Thumbnail image URL | ## Use Cases 1. **Product Discovery**: Allow users to search for products by name, brand, or category 2. **E-commerce Search**: Implement search functionality in online stores 3. **Inventory Lookup**: Find specific products in the catalog quickly 4. **Product Comparison**: Search for similar products to compare features and prices 5. **Mobile App Integration**: Power search features in mobile shopping applications 6. **Autocomplete/Suggestions**: Build search suggestion features based on partial queries ## Example Usage ### Search for phones ``` GET https://dummyjson.com/products/search?q=phone ``` ### Search for electronics ``` GET https://dummyjson.com/products/search?q=electronics ``` ### Search by brand ``` GET https://dummyjson.com/products/search?q=apple ``` ## Response Codes | Status Code | Description | | --- | --- | | 200 | Success - Returns matching products | | 400 | Bad Request - Invalid query parameter | | 404 | Not Found - No products match the search query | | 500 | Internal Server Error | ## Notes - The search is case-insensitive and searches across multiple fields (title, description, category, brand) - Results are returned with comprehensive product details including pricing, availability, and customer reviews - The endpoint supports pagination (check for `total`, `skip`, and `limit` fields in response)

Request Description
# Add New Product ## Description This endpoint allows you to add a new product to the system. It accepts product details in the request body and returns the created product with a unique ID assigned by the server. ## Request Body Parameters The request body should be in JSON format with the following fields: | Parameter | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `title` | string | Yes | The name/title of the product | | `price` | number | Yes | The price of the product (numeric value) | | `category` | string | Yes | The category the product belongs to (e.g., "electronics", "clothing", etc.) | ### Example Request Body ``` json { "title": "HTU brief assignment", "price": 150, "category": "electronics" } ``` ## Response ### Success Response **Status Codes:** - `200 OK` - Product created successfully - `201 Created` - Product created successfully (preferred status code) **Response Body:** The API returns the created product object with an auto-generated `id` field along with all the submitted product details. ``` json { "id": 195, "title": "HTU brief assignment", "price": 150, "category": "electronics" } ``` ### Response Fields | Field | Type | Description | | --- | --- | --- | | `id` | number | Unique identifier assigned to the product by the server | | `title` | string | The product title as submitted | | `price` | number | The product price as submitted | | `category` | string | The product category as submitted | ## Notes - The endpoint typically responds within 1000ms under normal conditions - The server automatically generates a unique `id` for each new product - All fields in the request body are required for successful product creation - The response includes all submitted data along with the generated product ID

Iteration: 1 - Update Product Price Only
Request Description
This endpoint allows you to update **only the price** of a specific product without modifying any other product attributes. It uses the PATCH method for partial updates. ## HTTP Method **PATCH** - Used for partial resource updates. Unlike PUT which replaces the entire resource, PATCH only modifies the specified fields. ## Endpoint ``` PATCH https://dummyjson.com/products/{id} ``` ## Path Parameters | Parameter | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `id` | integer | Yes | The unique identifier of the product whose price you want to update | ## Request Body The request body should be in JSON format containing only the price field. **Content-Type:** `application/json` ### Required Fields | Field | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `price` | number | Yes | The new price for the product (can be integer or decimal) | ### Example Request Body ``` json { "price": 999 } ``` ## Response Format Upon successful update, the API returns a **200 OK** status with the complete product object including the updated price. ### Example Response ``` json { "id": 1, "title": "Essence Mascara Lash Princess", "price": 999, "discountPercentage": 10.48, "stock": 99, "rating": 2.56, "brand": "Essence", "category": "beauty", "description": "The Essence Mascara Lash Princess is a...", "images": ["..."], "thumbnail": "..." } ``` ## Use Case Example **Scenario:** An e-commerce platform needs to quickly adjust product pricing during a flash sale or price correction without affecting other product details like description, stock, or images. **Action:** Send a PATCH request to update only the price field from $13.99 to $9.99 for product ID 1. **Benefit:** This approach is more efficient than sending all product data with a PUT request, reducing bandwidth and preventing accidental overwrites of other fields.

Request Description
# Delete Product This endpoint deletes a product from the system by its unique product ID. ## URL Structure ``` DELETE https://dummyjson.com/products/{id} ``` ### Path Parameters | Parameter | Type | Required | Description | | --- | --- | --- | --- | | `id` | integer | Yes | The unique identifier of the product to delete | **Example:** `https://dummyjson.com/products/1` deletes the product with ID 1. ## Response Format The API returns the complete product object that was deleted, including all its details along with deletion metadata. ### Success Response (200 OK) ``` json { "id": 1, "title": "Product Name", "description": "Product description", "category": "category-name", "price": 9.99, "discountPercentage": 10.48, "rating": 2.56, "stock": 99, "tags": ["tag1", "tag2"], "brand": "Brand Name", "sku": "SKU-CODE", "weight": 4, "dimensions": { "width": 15.14, "height": 13.08, "depth": 22.99 }, "warrantyInformation": "Warranty details", "shippingInformation": "Shipping details", "availabilityStatus": "Status", "reviews": [...], "returnPolicy": "Return policy details", "minimumOrderQuantity": 48, "meta": { "createdAt": "timestamp", "updatedAt": "timestamp", "barcode": "barcode", "qrCode": "qr-code-url" }, "images": ["image-urls"], "thumbnail": "thumbnail-url", "isDeleted": true, "deletedOn": "2026-01-29T14:49:02.616Z" } ``` ### Key Response Fields - **isDeleted**: Boolean flag set to `true` confirming the product has been deleted - **deletedOn**: ISO 8601 timestamp indicating when the product was deleted - All other fields contain the product's data at the time of deletion ## Status Codes | Status Code | Description | | --- | --- | | 200 OK | Product successfully deleted. Returns the deleted product object with `isDeleted: true` | | 404 Not Found | Product with the specified ID does not exist | | 401 Unauthorized | Authentication required or invalid credentials | | 403 Forbidden | User does not have permission to delete products | ## Automated Tests This request includes the following automated tests that run after receiving the response: 1. **Status Code Validation**: Verifies the response status code is 200 2. **Deletion Confirmation**: Checks that the `isDeleted` field in the response is `true` and logs the deleted product ID 3. **Performance Check**: Ensures the response time is less than 1000ms All tests must pass for the deletion to be considered successful. ## Usage Notes - This is a **destructive operation** - use with caution - The response includes the full product details for audit/logging purposes - The product ID in the URL must be a valid integer - Consider implementing soft deletes (as shown by the `isDeleted` flag) rather than hard deletes for data integrity

Iteration: 1 - Get carts
Request Description
This endpoint retrieves cart information from the DummyJSON API. It returns a paginated list of shopping carts with detailed product information, pricing, and discount calculations. ## Response Structure The response contains the following main fields: - **carts** (array): An array of cart objects containing all cart data - **total** (number): The total number of carts available - **skip** (number): The number of carts skipped (for pagination) - **limit** (number): The maximum number of carts returned per request ## Cart Object Structure Each cart in the `carts` array contains: - **id** (number): Unique identifier for the cart - **products** (array): Array of product objects in the cart - **total** (number): Total price of all products before discounts - **discountedTotal** (number): Total price after applying all discounts - **userId** (number): ID of the user who owns this cart - **totalProducts** (number): Number of distinct products in the cart - **totalQuantity** (number): Total quantity of all items in the cart ## Product Object Structure Each product within a cart contains: - **id** (number): Unique product identifier - **title** (string): Product name/title - **price** (number): Unit price of the product - **quantity** (number): Number of units of this product in the cart - **total** (number): Total price for this product (price quantity) - **discountPercentage** (number): Discount percentage applied to this product - **discountedTotal** (number): Total price after discount - **thumbnail** (string): URL to the product's thumbnail image ## Usage Notes - The endpoint returns a default of 30 carts per request (configurable via query parameters) - All monetary values are in decimal format - Discounts are calculated per product and then aggregated at the cart level - The `totalQuantity` represents the sum of all product quantities in the cart - Each cart is associated with a specific user via the `userId` field ## Example Use Cases - Retrieve all active shopping carts for analysis - Monitor cart abandonment rates - Calculate total revenue potential from pending carts - Analyze product popularity based on cart contents

Iteration: 1 - add carts
Request Description
## Overview This endpoint adds one or more products to a shopping cart. It creates a new cart entry with the specified products and calculates totals including any applicable discounts. ## Request Body The request requires a JSON payload with the following structure: ``` json { "userId": 5, "products": [ { "id": 1, "quantity": 2 } ] } ``` ### Required Fields | Field | Type | Description | | --- | --- | --- | | `userId` | integer | The unique identifier of the user adding items to cart | | `products` | array | Array of product objects to add to the cart | | `products[].id` | integer | The unique identifier of the product | | `products[].quantity` | integer | The quantity of the product to add | ## Response Format Upon successful cart creation, the API returns a `201 Created` status with a comprehensive cart object: ``` json { "id": 51, "products": [ { "id": 1, "title": "Essence Mascara Lash Princess", "price": 9.99, "quantity": 2, "total": 19.98, "discountPercentage": 10.48, "discountedPrice": 18, "thumbnail": "https://cdn.dummyjson.com/product-images/..." } ], "total": 19.98, "discountedTotal": 18, "userId": 5, "totalProducts": 1, "totalQuantity": 2 } ``` ### Response Fields | Field | Type | Description | | --- | --- | --- | | `id` | integer | Unique identifier for the created cart | | `products` | array | Detailed array of products with enriched information | | `products[].id` | integer | Product identifier | | `products[].title` | string | Product name/title | | `products[].price` | number | Unit price of the product | | `products[].quantity` | integer | Quantity added to cart | | `products[].total` | number | Subtotal (price quantity) | | `products[].discountPercentage` | number | Discount percentage applied | | `products[].discountedPrice` | number | Final price after discount | | `products[].thumbnail` | string | URL to product thumbnail image | | `total` | number | Cart total before discounts | | `discountedTotal` | number | Cart total after all discounts applied | | `userId` | integer | User ID associated with the cart | | `totalProducts` | integer | Count of unique products in cart | | `totalQuantity` | integer | Total quantity of all items in cart | ## Example Use Cases ### Single Product Addition Add one product with a specific quantity to create a new cart: ``` json { "userId": 5, "products": [{"id": 1, "quantity": 2}] } ``` ### Multiple Products Addition Add multiple different products in a single request: ``` json { "userId": 5, "products": [ {"id": 1, "quantity": 2}, {"id": 10, "quantity": 1}, {"id": 25, "quantity": 3} ] } ``` ### Bulk Quantity Order Add a large quantity of a single product: ``` json { "userId": 5, "products": [{"id": 1, "quantity": 50}] } ``` ## Important Notes - **userId**: Must be a valid user identifier in the system. The response will echo back this userId for verification. - **products array**: Can contain multiple product objects. Each product requires both `id` and `quantity` fields. - **Server-side calculations**: The server automatically enriches the response with product details (title, price, thumbnail) and calculates totals, discounts, and summary counts. - **Discount handling**: Discounts are automatically applied by the server based on product-specific discount percentages. - **Response status**: Successful cart creation returns `201 Created` status code. - **Cart ID**: Each cart creation generates a unique cart ID that can be used for subsequent cart operations. ## Validation This endpoint includes automated tests that verify: - Response status is 200 or 201 - Cart is created with a unique ID - Response contains the correct number of products - Server calculations (totals, discounts) are accurate - User ID in response matches the request

Iteration: 1 - put to carts
Request Description
## Overview This endpoint updates an existing cart by merging new products or updating quantities of existing products. The merge operation allows you to add products to the cart without replacing the entire cart contents. ## Endpoint ``` PUT https://dummyjson.com/carts/1 ``` ## Request Body Parameters ### `merge` (boolean) - **Required**: Yes - **Description**: Controls the merge behavior for the cart update - **Values**: - `true`: Merges the provided products with existing cart items. If a product already exists in the cart, its quantity will be updated. New products will be added. - `false`: Replaces the entire cart contents with the provided products ### `products` (array) - **Required**: Yes - **Description**: Array of product objects to add or update in the cart - **Structure**: Each product object contains: - `id` (number): The unique identifier of the product - `quantity` (number): The desired quantity for this product **Example Request Body:** ``` json { "merge": true, "products": [ { "id": 1, "quantity": 10 } ] } ``` ## Response Structure The API returns the updated cart object with the following structure: ``` json { "id": 1, "products": [ { "id": 168, "title": "Product Name", "price": 32999.99, "quantity": 3, "total": 98999.97, "discountPercentage": 13.39, "discountedPrice": 85744, "thumbnail": "https://..." } ], "total": 103874.75, "discountedTotal": 89775, "userId": 33, "totalProducts": 5, "totalQuantity": 25 } ``` ### Response Fields: - **id**: Cart identifier - **products**: Array of all products currently in the cart with full details - **total**: Sum of all product totals before discounts - **discountedTotal**: Total after applying all discounts - **userId**: ID of the user who owns this cart - **totalProducts**: Count of unique products in the cart - **totalQuantity**: Sum of quantities across all products ## Merge Behavior Notes 1. **Updating Existing Products**: When `merge: true` and a product with the specified ID already exists in the cart, only the quantity is updated. The product is not duplicated. 2. **Adding New Products**: Products with IDs not currently in the cart will be added as new items. 3. **Automatic Recalculation**: The API automatically recalculates: - Individual product totals (`price quantity`) - Cart total (sum of all product totals) - Discounted prices and totals - Total product count and quantity 4. **Replace Mode**: When `merge: false`, all existing cart items are removed and replaced with the products in the request. ## Status Codes - **200 OK**: Cart successfully updated - **400 Bad Request**: Invalid request body or parameters - **404 Not Found**: Cart with specified ID does not exist ## Testing This request includes automated tests that verify: - Response status is 200 - Product quantity is correctly updated to the specified value - Cart total is accurately recalculated - Response time is within acceptable limits (<800ms)

Iteration: 1 - delete carts
Request Description
This endpoint deletes a specific cart from the system using its unique identifier. ## Endpoint ``` DELETE https://dummyjson.com/carts/{id} ``` ## URL Structure The endpoint uses a path parameter to identify which cart to delete: - **`{id}`** (required) - The unique identifier of the cart to be deleted - Type: Integer - Example: `1` - Location: URL path ## Request No request body is required for this endpoint. Simply specify the cart ID in the URL path. ### Example Request ``` DELETE https://dummyjson.com/carts/1 ``` ## Response ### Success Response The API returns the deleted cart object with additional metadata confirming the deletion. **Status Codes:** - `200 OK` - Cart successfully deleted, returns the deleted cart details - `204 No Content` - Cart successfully deleted, no response body returned ### Response Body Structure (Status 200) ``` json { "id": 1, "products": [ { "id": 168, "title": "Product Name", "price": 32999.99, "quantity": 3, "total": 98999.97, "discountPercentage": 13.39, "discountedTotal": 85743.87, "thumbnail": "https://cdn.example.com/image.jpg" } ], "total": 103774.85, "discountedTotal": 89686.65, "userId": 33, "totalProducts": 4, "totalQuantity": 15, "isDeleted": true, "deletedOn": "2026-01-29T15:52:52.532Z" } ``` ### Response Fields | Field | Type | Description | | --- | --- | --- | | `id` | integer | The ID of the deleted cart | | `products` | array | Array of product objects that were in the cart | | `total` | number | Original total price before discounts | | `discountedTotal` | number | Total price after applying discounts | | `userId` | integer | ID of the user who owned the cart | | `totalProducts` | integer | Number of unique products in the cart | | `totalQuantity` | integer | Total quantity of all items in the cart | | `isDeleted` | boolean | Confirmation flag indicating the cart has been deleted (always `true`) | | `deletedOn` | string | ISO 8601 timestamp of when the cart was deleted | ## Deletion Behavior - The deletion is performed on the cart specified by the ID in the URL path - The response includes the complete cart details before deletion, along with deletion metadata - The `isDeleted` flag is set to `true` to confirm successful deletion - The `deletedOn` timestamp records the exact time of deletion - If the cart ID doesn't exist, the API may return an error response (implementation-dependent) ## Notes - This is a **destructive operation** - the cart and its contents will be removed from the system - The response provides a complete record of what was deleted, which can be useful for audit trails or undo functionality - Ensure you have proper authorization to delete the specified cart - The cart ID must match the user's cart or appropriate permissions must be in place
